     <script type="text/javascript">
      function GetSlickIndexForArticle() {
            var index = -1;
            var _hashValue = window.location.hash;
            if (_hashValue.indexOf("#a") == 0) {
                var _article = _hashValue.substring(2);
                var _image = $(".headlineNumeric.type01 img[data-id='" + _article + "']");
                index = _image.parents("li").index();
            }
            history.replaceState("", document.title, window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
            return index;
        }

        var slideTimer01 = 0;
        var currentItemFrontTop01 = GetSlickIndexForArticle();
        $('.headlineNumeric.type01 ul')
        .on('init', function (event, slick) {
            $('.slick-dots li', slick.$slider.parent()).unbind('click');

            SlickInitialize(slick.$slider.parent(), 1);

            if (slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current').hasClass('last-minute flash'))
                slick.$slider.find('.slick-slide.slick-current')
                             .find('a')
                             .append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="https://isbh.tmgrup.com.tr/sbh/site/v4/homepage/i/flas-flas.png" alt="" /></div>');

            if (currentItemFrontTop01 > -1) {
                $('body').addClass('socialExtraMain');

                if (currentItemFrontTop01 != 0) {
                    var $imgContainer = $(slick.$slides[currentItemFrontTop01]);
                    var $image = $imgContainer.find("img:first[data-src-real]");

                    if ($image) {
                        var imageSrc = $image.attr("data-src-real");

                        $image.attr("src", imageSrc)
                            .removeAttr("data-src-real")
                            .removeAttr("data-src");
                    }
                }
            }
        })
        .on('beforeChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide) {
            nextSlide == currentItemFrontTop01 ? $('body').addClass('socialExtraMain') : $('body').removeClass('socialExtraMain');

            if ($(slick.$slides[nextSlide]).hasClass('last-minute'))
                $(slick.$slides[nextSlide]).find('.slider-animation').remove();
        })
        .on('afterChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide) {
            if ($(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).hasClass('last-minute flash'))
                $(slick.$slides[currentSlide]).find('a').append('<div class="slider-animation"><img src="https://isbh.tmgrup.com.tr/sbh/site/v4/homepage/i/flas-flas.png" alt="" /></div>');

            if (GlobalVariables.MultiLazyLoad) {
                clearTimeout(slideTimer01);

                slideTimer01 = setTimeout(function () {
                    var $imgContainer = $(slick.$slides[currentSlide]);
                    var $image = $imgContainer.find("img:first[data-src-real]");
                    if ($image) {
                        var imageSrc = $image.attr("data-src-real");
                        if (imageSrc) {
                            var img = new Image();
                            //img.src = imageSrc;
                            img.onload = function (e, b, n) {
                                $image.attr("src", imageSrc)
                                    .removeAttr("data-src-real")
                                    .removeAttr("data-src");
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }, 300);
            }
        })
        .slick({
            dots: true,
            speed: 300,
            arrows: false,
            touchThreshold: 100,
            pauseOnDotsHover: true,
            customPaging: function (slider, i) {
                var _link = $('a', slider.$slides[i]).attr('href');
                return '<a target="_blank" href="' + _link + '">' + (i + 1) + '</a>';
            },
            initialSlide: (currentItemFrontTop01 < 0 ? 0 : currentItemFrontTop01)
        });
     </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function () {
        $.getJSON(unescape('/getsondakikabandasjson'), null, function (data) {
            var isIE = window.navigator.msPointerEnabled,
                _isIE = isIE ? false : true;

            if (data.Success && data.List.length > 0) {
                if (data.List.length % 2 != 0)
                    data.List.splice(data.List.length - 1, 1);

                var _title, _url, _date;

                var _itemHtml = '<ul class="items">';
                for (i = 0; i < data.List.length; i++) {
                    _title = data.List[i].Title;
                    _url = data.List[i].Url;
                    _date = data.List[i].Date;

                    _itemHtml += '<li>';
                    _itemHtml += '  <a title="{TITLE}" href="{URL}" target="_blank">'
                    _itemHtml += '      <i>{DATE}</i>';
                    _itemHtml += '      <em>{TITLE}</em>';
                    _itemHtml += '  </a>';
                    _itemHtml += '</li>';

                    _itemHtml = _itemHtml
                        .replace(/{TITLE}/g, _title)
                        .replace(/{URL}/g, _url)
                        .replace(/{DATE}/g, _date);
                }
                _itemHtml += '</ul>';

                $(".lastMinNews").append(_itemHtml);
                $(".lastMinNews").addClass("show");

                $('.lastMinNews ul').slick({
                    dots: false,
                    vertical: true,
                    infinite: true,
                    speed: 300,
                    slidesPerRow: 1,
                    rows: 3,
                    autoplay: _isIE,
                    autoplaySpeed: 3000,
                    arrows: false,
                    touchThreshold: 100,
                    pauseOnDotsHover: true,
                    touchThreshold: 100,
                    responsive: [{
                        breakpoint: 993,
                        settings: {
                            slidesToShow: 3,
                            slidesToScroll: 1,
                            slidesPerRow: 1,
                            rows: 2
                        }
                    }]
                });
            }
        });
    });
     </script>

         $(function () {
            var $ItemA, ts1A, ts2A, tabCtrlA = true;
            var exTabIndexA = 0;
            $('.sari-sayfalar-widget ul.tabs').find('li').each(function (index) {
                $(this).click(function () {
                    if (tabCtrlA && exTabIndexA != index) {
                        tabCtrlA = false;
                        if (exTabIndexA == 0) { ts1A = 0; ts2A = 1 }
                        else if (exTabIndexA == 1) {
                            if (index == 0) { ts1A = 1; ts2A = 0 }
                            else { ts1A = 0; ts2A = 1 }
                        }
                        else if (exTabIndexA == 2) { ts1A = 1; ts2A = 0 }
                        $('.sari-sayfalar-widget ul.tabs').find('li').removeClass('current');
                        $(this).addClass('current');
                        $('.sari-sayfalar-widget .cells .cell').hide();
                        $('.sari-sayfalar-widget .cells .cell').eq(index).fadeIn();
                        tabCtrlA = true;
                        exTabIndexA = index;
                    }
                });
            });
        });

      $('.liveChannelTab .tabMenu li').each(function (index) {
        $(this).click(function () {
            $('.liveChannelTab .tabMenu li').removeClass('selected')
            !$(this).hasClass('selected') ? $(this).addClass('selected') : undefined;
            $('.liveChannelTab .itemFrame').find('.item').removeClass('show').eq(index).addClass('show');
        })
    });
